<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meert</a> (64043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>Related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marter.html>marter</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language"><a href = vnd.unilang:west.html>West</a> Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">murd</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Groningen<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">polecat</span>
<ul><li><b>1914</b> February 2, "<a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>Over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dialect.html>Dialect</a>, XI.", <i>Nieuwsblad <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noorden.html>Noorden</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:second.html>second</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:part.html>part</a>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>Zit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> „<b><a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meert</a></b>” <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:benauwdheid.html>benauwdheid</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoot.html>stoot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> allerakeligste <a href = vnd.unilang:klanken.html>klanken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1929</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:march.html>March</a> 16, "<a href = vnd.unilang:praatje.html>Praatjes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaatjes.html>plaatjes</a>", <i>Nieuwsblad <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noorden.html>Noorden</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:third.html>third</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:part.html>part</a>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:misschien.html>Misschien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:indertijd.html>indertijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> boederijtje <a href = vnd.unilang:gestaan.html>gestaan</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> „<b><a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meerten</a></b>” <a href = vnd.unilang:veelvuldig.html>veelvuldig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorkwamen.html>voorkwamen</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1934</b> January 27, "<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> veldmuizenplaag. <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nuttige.html>nuttige</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meert</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzing</a>.", <i>Nieuwsblad <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noorden.html>Noorden</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:seventh.html>seventh</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:part.html>part</a>.</li>
<li><b>1976</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:september.html>September</a> 6, "Sportaccommodatie <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> oosthoek <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Kollumerland <a href = vnd.unilang:sterk.html>sterk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbeterd.html>verbeterd</a>", <i>Leeuwarder <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>Courant</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:page.html>page</a> 23.

***meid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a> (700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meit</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:variant.html>variant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meget</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*megith</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*magath</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*magaþs</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maagd.html>maagd</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
